### Post by Samhain13 on 2007-10-06
> **Jucato said:**
> Oy Samhain nasan ang mga detalye mo? :)

Detalye ko? Hummm...

Web Designer mula sa Pasig.

Gumagamit ng: X/HTML, CSS, Javascript, PHP at MySQL (minsan). Gumagawa din minsan ng Graphic Design, FLASH, MIDI at konting Video Editing.

Tumatangkilik sa Web Standards at Accessibility,
at sa awa ng Diyos, nakilala na ng DSWD, NCC-CICT at kamakailan lang, ng [Accessites](http://accessites.org/site/2007/10/arielle-b-cruz/). Nabanggit din ang mga gawa ko sa aklat na "Basic Web Accessibility Guide for Filipinos" na isinulat ni Remberto Esposa, Jr, At nakapagsalita na din tungkol sa Multimedia Arts sa De La Salle University - College of Saint Benilde.

Kulang-kulang nang isang taong gumagamit ng Ubuntu at nananatiling maligaya sa paggamit nito.

Tumutulong din sa pagsasalin sa Tagalog ng mga application sa pamamagitan ng [Launchpad](https://launchpad.net/~arielle-cruz).

Ayun. :D

### Post by Johnaray on 2007-10-07
MABUHAY!

Ako po ay isang hamak lamang na trabahador mula sa Makati, ngunit ang aking bahay ay sa Paco, Manila.

Nagtapos ako sa kursong Enhinyero ng komputer.

Bagama't isa akong baguhan sa larangan ng paggamit sa UBUNTU LINUX bilang pangunahing sistema pang operasyon ng komputer, ako naman ay mayroon ding kakarampot na kaalaman ukol sa paggamit nang naturang sistemang pang operasyon ng komputer.

Sa ngayon ay isa din akong Tagapamagitan (Moderator) ng isang FORUM na ang pangalan ay NEXTCODE.INFO, sa ngayon ang aking adhikain ay ang maikalat ang kaalaman ukol sa libreng sistemang pang operasyon ng komputer at dahil dyan ay isa ako sa mga masugid na sumusuporta sa UBUNTU LINUX.

Muli po sana ay magtulungan po tayo at nawa'y adyain ng maykapal na minsan tayo ay magkadalaupang palad lahat.

MABUHAY TAYONG LAHAT!!!

### Post by zakame on 2007-10-08
Awesome to see this rolling nicely and finally, hehe :D

I'm Zak, from Daet, Camarines Norte.  I'm the one who requested this forum, being the LoCoTeam contact for Ubuntu-PH, after some good-natured persuasion from the community (in the mailing list and IRC.) :D  I'm also the guy to contact with if you want large shipments of Ubuntu CDs (only with good reason, hehe. :P)

Along with Jerome Gotangco, Irvin Piraman, Aldous Peñaranda, Dax Umaming,  and Juan Carlos Torres, we make up the team of recognized Ubuntu Community Members (e.g. the card-carrying Ubunteros with the @ubuntu.com email address.)  And I want YOU guys to join our merry band of Ubunteros, to help out in Ubuntu development in various areas (packaging, documentation, translations, even training. ;)  See [http://www.ubuntu.com/community/participate](http://www.ubuntu.com/community/participate) to know how. :D

Among things other than Ubuntu, I dabble with a lot of technologies other than Linux; more recently my new job has gotten me into the world of Macs (just another UNIX, really, ;) Perl and Ruby application development (Rails and Catalyst rocks,) and grid virtualization (anyone playing with Plan 9 or Inferno here?)  I also have been fortunate to work with OSDL (now the Linux Foundation) in last year's Google Summer of Code.  And I haven't even worked out a college degree yet. :P

Anyway, enough of my babble!  If you want more, just catch me in the #ubuntu-ph IRC channel on FreeNode. :D I'll make it a point to check the forums every now and then for interesting tidbits, too.

More power to Ubuntu and the Filipino people!

Zakame

### Post by delphiguy on 2007-10-21
wow, ngayon ko lang nalaman na me local group pala ng Ubuntu sa atin, buti na lang nag
google ako.

Anyways, Ubuntu user ako since na release ung Dapper Drake (6.10), and sa lahat ng 
distro ng Linux ito ang pinakanagustuhan ko.  Ang love affair ko sa Linux eh on and off, 
from Red Hat, Caldera, Mandrake, Corel, Fedora, Mandriva, DreamLinux, Sabayon. and 
now Ubuntu, at sa Ubuntu lang ako nag stick, kasi napakadali nyang gamitin, at ang 
community support eh napaka husay.

At magmula nga nung nagamit ko ung Ubuntu, exclusive OS ko na sya sa bahay, wala kang 
makikitang Windows OS na, until recently lang nung nag ka project ako na ang requirement
eh Windows application, so ung laptop ko nilagyan ko ng Vista at dual boot ng Ubuntu.
Hindi kasi kaya ng loob ko na mag install ng Linux sa vmware, pakiramdam ko eh binabastos
ko ang Linux.

Marami pa akong dapat matutunan sa linux, sana magkaroon tayo ng Conference or 
seminars para sa ikakaunlad ng Philippine Linux Community.

BTW, Randy po, and programmer, however puros Windows development palang at the
moment nag aaral pa akong mag linux programming eh (huhuhuh), wala kasing oras.

Salamat po.

LOL..I'm fully aware of that, that's why I try not to call myself an otaku as much as possible (though I actually am one, and I've been called an "otaku" by a Japanese before, LOL). ### Post by youtin on 2008-03-01
> **sonnydoriginal said:**
> Pastor Sonny dela Peña
Yahoomail- [email]Sonnydoriginal@yahoo.com[/email]
Cureently using microsoft windows xp
I'm planniing to switch to Linux-kubuntu
could you give me an idea regarding linux and benefits

As for me the best benefit po is that hindi na kailangang mag-worry about viruses (from personal experience, 99% of computers in the Phils are infected with viruses). Aside from that,it's free and you can rest your conscience knowing that you are not participating in piracy (original Microsoft products are very expensive). I think the organization of Linux OSes are also better because they don't bog down like Windows over time (for many years I would reformat Windows XP every few months because of virus issues and loss of performance).

### Post by benhur99ph on 2008-06-06
Mabuhay!!!

Wow! I'm ashamed to say that I have been using Ubuntu since 6.06 and I haven't been here before. I've always been an avid fan of Linux ever since I tried Ubuntu 6.06. It opened a whole new world for me and I've been using it up to now.

I don't know what prompted me to search for an Ubuntu Community that's local, but to my surprise, when I did, I found this forum! I am very happy to see that there are so many of us who like to use this wondrous operating system. Ubuntu has really come far in the past few years and I'm proud to say that I have been using it as my main operating system for sometime now. I still use windows, but only for web development, mainly using the Adobe Creative Suit. I have heard that Adobe works with wine but I'd rather use my Windows Xp as a virtual machine running on my Ubuntu (via virtualbox)because it just works better for me. 

Sorry if I talked to much, I was just overwhelmed by the fact that there are many of us, Filipinos, who share the same passion that I have. Anyways, I'm ben, 23 years young, an Ubuntu user. I'm glad to meet all of you!

### Post by rqmpo on 2008-06-19
Matagal na ako dito pransiya, pero Pinoy pa rin ako at heart. Dati akong sysad dito sa Paris bago ako napatigil ng trabaho for health reasons. Financial resources permitting, umuuwi ako sa Pinas for a few months once every year or two years. Bilang dating sysad, exposed ako sa Unix ( nineteen forgotten ) but I have been a regular and fulltime Linux user since about five years. About three years back, I attended a national IT conference in Bacolod. I found out that, at that time, Linux was only for UP, Ateneo and La Salle engineering guys. Natutuwa ako that today bumibilis ang pagkalat ng Ubuntu at opensource sa Pinas, in some cases, even reaching schools in far-flung areas. More success to this and other open source forums.

### Post by garylamanilao on 2008-06-24
Gary here. Been using 8.04 (Hardy Heron) as my main OS for 2 months +/- and lovin' the d@mn thing. I would have switched since 6.06 but during that time I just didn't have the patience to "unlearn" decades of MS interface (from MS DOS 5 - though I'm not really that old).

Shift from MS to Ubuntu is just a matter of will, difficult at first to learn which-is-what specially if you're bound by MS interface. I'm no Ubuntu expert, but if someone is starting from scratch (no MS experience) I think the interface is a lot easier to grow with... specially with MS Vista's over-sophistication. Took me a week or so to get familiar with the conventions, after that work is more efficient (than XP or Vista). Although I still don't like the going thru "terminal" and typing "sudo ____ "... too complicated for me, and I'm just that lazy I think. Glad I don't have to do them unless I have to install certain applications like JDK or Oracle XE that I think are not in the repositories list.

Short comings would be unfamiliar fonts, I really grew up with either Tahoma or Arial. I guess these are MS properties. So no hope here I guess.

Another would be lack of stand-alone Accounting programs (like Peachtree or Quickbooks), I understand that there are available open-source programs available out there (Timy-erp, Openbravo, etc.) that are great - but they're just difficult to implement (dependencies to JDK, Oracle XE, Apache, etc.). Closest I've seen so far is P2P Account by Samooha, although they're still on beta and work seems to be hampered. I remember a local project "elohai" ([www.elohai.livejournal.com](www.elohai.livejournal.com)) though like samooha, there's just lack of activity on that build. Still researching on how to mobilize Openbravo, overkill for my business requirements, but it should suffice. If only JDK and Oracle XE wasn't that hard to implement. "sigh"

Enough ranting, Ubuntu is an excellent OS. All it needs is a simple accounting program and probably a counterpart for MS Direct X. Again, I'm no expert, just ranting and appreciating an excellent OS. :)

---

### Post by wersdaluv on 2008-06-26
> **garylamanilao said:**
> Short comings would be unfamiliar fonts, I really grew up with either Tahoma or Arial. I guess these are MS properties. So no hope here I guess.

You can install MS fonts (even the ones in office 2007 but I don't know if it's legal). Here's something legal-> [http://ubuntu.wordpress.com/2005/09/09/installing-microsoft-fonts/](http://ubuntu.wordpress.com/2005/09/09/installing-microsoft-fonts/) (I think). 

One important thing that I learned when I switched to Ubuntu is to maximize Google. After some months, I figured out that whenever I have something to fix in mind, I shouldn't hesitate googling. 

I would also say that I hated the terminal before but I'm loving it now. You just have to understand what those codes mean then after some time, you'll get used to them. Start with finding out what **sudo**, **apt-get**, and **cd** are. 

Good luck.

hello po, mga cho-karan!

laking Pampanga...pero nasa San Francisco, California, USA na po!
kumusta po kayong lahat diyan.

(Kapangpangan): Mayap a aldo kekayo ngan!
(English): Good day to you all!

May personal project po akong gagawin sa pagbalik ko ng Pilipinas.
Ang balak ko po ay ma-iangat natin ang edukasyon sa Pilipinas, lalo na sa mga estudyanteng nasa mababang paaralan.

Ka-awa-awa ang kanilang kalagayan.
Napagiwanan na sila ng panahon.
Hindi makatulong ang gubyerno ng Pilipinas sa larangan ng pag-angat ng estado ng pambansang edukasyon.

Ang dapat gawain ay makapagsimula ng isang grupo na nasa pribadong sektor na ang layunin ay makapagbigay ng edukason de kalidad gamit ng mga lumang computers na may UBUNTU ang operating system.

Susuportahan ko po ang sinumang makapagsimula ng grupong ito.
May kakayahan akong makatulong sa pamamagitan ng paghanap ng suportang pinansyal at "administrative and executive support"

Sana nawa ay matupad itong munting kahilingan para makatulong sa ating mga kabataan.

Nang-gagalang,

matagal na po akong gumagamit ng linux, ngunit ngayon lang ako gumamit ng ubuntu. ang makinang gamit ko po ay acer aspire one (d150), na nagpapatakbo ng Jaunty UNR.

masasabi ko pong ako ay may konting kaalaman sa programming at pagsy-sysad.

maraming salamat po, at mainam na itaguyod ang ph.ubuntuforums para sa ating mga kababayan.

(ps: inabot ako ng mahigit limang minuto para isulat ang inisaad ko sa itaas. karaniwang ginawaga ko lang ng isang minuto kung gagamit ng wikang banyaga. nakatutuwa na ako'y napa-isip ng husto.)

### Post by PINOY_RADICAL on 2009-05-03

mga kababayan. mawalang galang na ho. pinost ko po ang tanong kong ito sa Pinoy Ubuntu users thread. nais ko rin itong ipost dito.

patulong naman po mga *expert*,

'pag ginagawa kong *livecd* yung *ubuntu8.10* sa *laptop* ko walang *higher resolutions available*.

> ubuntu@ubuntu:~$ xrandr
Screen 0: minimum 640 x 480, current 800 x 600, maximum 800 x 600
default connected 800x600+0+0 0mm x 0mm
800x600 61.0*
640x480 60.0
ubuntu@ubuntu:~$ xrandr -s 1280x800
Size 1280x800 not found in available modes
ubuntu@ubuntu:~$ 


wala yung *resolution* na 1280x800 para sakanya.
ano ang dapat gawin para makuha yung tamang *resolution* para sa a*cer aspire 4220*?

nawa'y matulungan ninyo ako sa aking problema mga kababayan.
baguhan lamang akong gumagamit ng Linux.

### Post by rozzpalacio76 on 2009-05-17
):P 

Hi Guys, Rozz Palacio is the name. A wannabee ubuntu'ers. Mga 6 months ko palang nae-experience ang ubunutu OS. Im using dual boot both in my laptop and desktop. Im beginning to love ubuntu. Right now Im self studying Ubuntu 8.04 server thru ebook. Happy to see more and more pinoys started using ubuntu. Meaming di lang akong nag-iisang pinoy ang nag-open ng 3rd eye for free OS without using pirated copy of OS. Mabuhay Ang Mga Ubuntu'ers na PINOY !  

My Desktop

CPU : AMD Athlon 64bit
MOBO : Gigabyte
RAM: 6Gig DDR2 Dual Channel 128-bit
Video: built-in HDMI
HD : 1X500Gig SATA, 1X160Gig SATA, 1X80Gig SATA all seagate
Monitor : Low tech na 19"AOC di makalusot kay misis ng 32" LCD
OS : Dual Boot Ubunut 8.10 & Windows Vista

Laptop Specs

Dell Inspiron 1300
RAM : 512MB
HD : 80Gig Samsung
OS : Dual Boot Ubuntu 8.10 & Windows XP SP2

Sorry Guys Mas Napakilala ko yung PC kesa sa akin. Hehehehe

BTW ako si Rozz Palacio, May Asawa na at madalas napapagalitan coz inu-umaga sa harap ng PC ko.
33 yrs old & computer addict. Taga Rizal,Laguna & Cavite po ang inyong lingkod. Meralco Foundation Graduate ng Electronics. Mula ng nagkaPC ako di na ako natahimik sa keyboard. One thing for sure I LOVEEEEEE PC and NOW UBUNTU COZ kahit wala akong ANTI-VIRUZZZZZ walang problema.

Hi Tope, if you really can't escape from MSOffice just like me, then you have two option. First you install VirtualBox in your ubuntu, you can have multiple OS inside Ubuntu or 2nd Option install Crossover equivalent to Wine, Im running MSOffice2003 at my ubuntu 8.10 syempre may mga limititation like MACRO & VB, but other than that OK na OK sya. Try mo lang baka magustuhan mo.

### Post by OnesimusUnbound on 2009-06-17

### Post by jaceleon on 2009-10-12
Ace Leon po!
I'm still young (as in wala sa face at body ang age) looking, isang normal (daw?) na bantay sa isang computer shop sa San Andres Bukid at isang techie enthusiast (totally on Windows XP, Vista, and7), at nagkataon na napagtripan ko ang Ubuntu Hardy Heron four days ago. <sound effect: Hallelujah!>

Sinimulan ko to sa pagdownload ng Ubuntu Hardy sa web. then gamit ako UNetbootin para gawa ng Live Version, and <sound effect: BOOM!> I fall in love agad! Sobrang secure!

Di tinopak na naman ako. Gawa ulit sa UNetbootin ng Live version, pero this time, Jaunty na! Mas na-inlove ako <sound effect: fireworks display nung bagong taon sa mayamang kapitbahay>, mas slick!

Eto ang ginawa ko tuloy - nireformat ko computer na gamit ko (yung spare lang na pakalat-kalat) at tapos ininstall ko na, and I may say, wala na akong balak palitan ito ng OS (except sa parating na Karmic Koala)

By the way, nagbabasa ako ng tungkol dito sa Ubuntu Karmic release party, kailan po yan? Saan po? May I come po?

Also, sino naman po may manual sa lahat ng commands sa Terminal? Pahiram naman po, please?!? Mas prefer ko kasi gamitin ang terminal kesa sa Add/Remove at Synaptics e.

**ATI Rage Ultra graphics card with 32MB of VRAM**

If this is the spec of your PC, try upgrading your Graphic Card Driver from ATI. 

[http://support.amd.com/us/gpudownload/Pages/index.aspx](http://support.amd.com/us/gpudownload/Pages/index.aspx)

Not sure of this but usually, freezing is because of the graphics card driver.

Hope this helps.

### Post by sagitta on 2009-11-04
Mabuhau Alex here!
Comp Sci student from Cebu.
Linux user for 1 year.

First ko gamit ng Ubuntu(my first Linux Distro) was when I was given an Ubuntu 8.04 LiveCD by one of the trainers at TESDA where I took a PC technician course.

Napaka-bumpy ng first impressions ko with using Ubuntu, especially when I was frustrated na hindi ma enable ang Desktop-effects, which the problem I traced to Linux not properly detecting my monitor's proper Sync and Refresh rates.  From there it was self-study, trial and error and "when-all-else-fails-consult-the-forums" learning linux.  Hindi ko na nga maalala kung ilang beses ako nag-reformat/re-install dahil sa mga kamalian ko.

Currently using Linux Mint 7, despite my attempts to try yung ibang mga distro I find it hard to acclimatize to their environments, probably because Ubuntu impacted so that I really am tied down to it...

Oh yeah, isa sa mga rason na na-astigan ako sa Linux...

I comes with a C compiler yung gcc(which back then I was just starting to learn :p )

-cheers!

### Post by vhinz on 2009-12-03
Elow poh,

Vincent po and working in Makati. I have been trying Linux for the nth time but have been seriously using it since this year and installed Ubuntu on my laptop last March. 

Still MS user in the office and wherever (puro Windows dito sa atin and I've always been tagged to help friends with their computers).

I first tried Bayanihan Linux years back even before v.2 but never got far enough because I don't know what to do with it.  But with my recent experience with Ubuntu last year made me install it on my laptop this year erasing Windows from it completely.

My laptop was built for Vista and therefore no XP drivers.  Not putting Vista on it and I have not been using pirated software anymore.  Ubuntu simply worked like a charm with one exception of wireless but upon research, I uninstalled Network Manager and replaced it with wicd and it started working.  Also a few searches have made our Globe Tatoo working as well.

My wife complained that she doesn't know how to use it esp. games but when she got used to it, she never complained...anyways, she's addicted to facebook, farmville and cafeworld.

BTW, I also influenced my wife's cousin and he and his children are using it from May.  They have installed it on P4 laptop and just upgraded to Karmic.

---

### Post by jaceleon on 2009-12-04
Welcome po kuya Vhinz!

So far, I got the impression that you are convincing other people to switch. Okay yan ah!

Ubuntu and all Ubuntu-based distros are good, kanya kanya ng advantage. I use Ubuntu 9.10 on my desktop as testing ground, 9.04 for compatibility at #! Linux sa laptop ko for speed, since luma na rin laptop ko.

In the case of computers having no driver because of it being especially built for Vista or 7 (your case) or drivers are now obsolete (my case), Ubuntu is a good choice if you don't want to go the "Dark Corridor of Piracy":P

In the end, depende sa iyo if what distro will you choose, we'll just be here to help out.

Welcome again, kuya!

### Post by jaceleon on 2009-12-08
Kuya Vhinz, malapit ka lang pala dito sa place ko e. Dito ako sa may San Andres Bukid.

Actually, kung Microsoft Office lang ang application na hindi mo maiwanan along windows, I already posted a guide on how to install MS Office 200X(2000, 2003 and 2007) in Ubuntu. Click [here]("http://ubuntuforums.org/showthread.php?t=1326164").

Apart from that, I can (sa kaso ko ah) run 80% of all my necessary Windows Applications na needed ko like RPG Maker 2k/3/VX/XP (Game-Creating Engine for Windows, each version for an OS of Windows e.g. 2k for 2000/NT/ME, 2k3 for server 2003, XP for XP and VX for Vista and XP), Valkyrie Profile Tag Battle (Doujinshi game ng sikat na Valkyrie Profile Series ng Square-Enix na tekken-styled), Warcraft III (DOTA pare, at pwede maglaban via LAN with windows users), Counter-Strike, O2mania (O2Jam Offline) pati na rin ePSXe (PS1 emulator). Just use wine, get the latest winetricks and playonlinux.

Microsoft is not the only way to run Windows-based application. Just use wine, and if in doubt if a certain app wont work, look on wine's database of application compatibility.

---

### Post by jaceleon on 2009-12-09
@vhinz

Ah, themes ba? okay din yan.

About sa post 758 ng desktop pix, yung post ko, it is conky that is being on the right side (yung puro system monitoring at statistics). I just disabled the usual theme of gnome and used the openbox interface (installed Openbox, logged out then used Openbox as session in login screen), openbox is something like gnome (default ubuntu theme), kde (default kubuntu theme) and XFCE (xubuntu default), pero hindi siya Desktop environment. try installing openbox and add the crunchbang linux repository to get their default conky theme, though pwede ka rin kumuha sa main ubuntu repository ng conky. By the way, Openbox is actually making your resources much faster and snappy in loading, since it disables the GNOME, KDE and XFCE to its very lightweight (and very technical) theming system. Kung yung Conky lang ang gusto mo roon, just install it from the repos. Then search for a very good Conky script in google. Kaya lang sa openbox, ang start ay nasa right-click, walang icons sa desktop (very neat and no clutters) at simple lang. No eye candy there, except sa nakakabaliw na conky (very customizable yan, pwede mo ipa-indicate kahit ano ata)

kung gusto mo naman ng total transformation ng Ubuntu to certain other Operating System themes (Windows 98, XP, Vista, Seven, Mac OSX, XP Media Edition, etc.), I suggest na ibigay mo sa akin email mo for me to send you the repository of the themes in .deb from Cyvoc OS, Ubuntu-based din yan, bago lang (created last November) at ang purpose niyan ay para mapadali ang transition ng mga other operating system users to Ubuntu by making gnome take the look of the OS it tries to imitate. as in ginawa niyang Windows 7 ang look ng Desktop ko kahit Pentium III lang yun, at halos weightless sa resources ang theming system niya. [here']("http://ubuntuforums.org/showthread.php?t=1337517")s the link if you want to see the screenies.

I know many would suggest sticking to the main system's rule, pero it's not that bad na mag-explorer ng others. After all, Ubuntu is customizable at pwede ka mag mix and match (basta ask for advise).

---

### Post by zeroseven0183 on 2010-10-26
Welcome to all newcomers!

Feel free to post your questions, ideas, suggestions, comments and screenshots on our forum.

Visit our [Local Community team page]("http://loco.ubuntu.com/teams/loco-philippine-team") for more information about Ubuntu Team Philippines.

You may also want to subscribe to our [mailing list]("https://lists.ubuntu.com/mailman/listinfo/ubuntu-ph"). *(Don't worry, low volume lang 'to ng mga e-mails. Promise!)*

And of course, our team website [http://ubuntu-ph.org/.]("http://ubuntu-ph.org/")

Kung wala pang [Launchpad]("https://launchpad.net/") account, we suggest you have one too and [magjoin na rin]("https://launchpad.net/%7Eloco-philippine-team").
Anyway, lahat naman ng mga ito ay LIBRE as in FREE!

:p

### Post by franchoy on 2011-02-26
[HTML][/HTML]> **loell said:**

yah i know, what im just saying is that mas significant yung help na makukuha mo sa forum kasi mas specific ung pinagtatanungan mo, mas concentrated ung tao sa forum. Well at least for my experience. Kasi ilang beses na kong na-isnob sa irc... may incident pa nga noon na sinabihan ako ng admin na di supported sa irc ung ung gusto kong gawin kasi nag-shift ako sa BURG from GRUB... I felt offended kaya nun... :( I know di sila binabayaran pero sa mga newbie kasi kailangan nila ng lahat ng support na makukuha nila, at sana may magsilbing parang mga big brother nila sa mga communities tulad nito...

### Post by zeroseven0183 on 2011-03-08
> **gl1tch said:**
> Hi guys new here..

i want to learn the world of linux! bow. 

IT Manager po ako ng isang company pero lahat ng softwares namin is Win. yun lang

We're glad to know you're on board, sir. We suggest you start reading Ubuntu Manual to familiarize yourself with Ubuntu and Linux. You can download a free copy of it at [http://ubuntu-manual.org/](http://ubuntu-manual.org/)

Second, keep in touch with the Philippine Team here in Ubuntu Forums. Feel free to post your questions and suggestions. Siguradong may sasagot ng mga tanong mo dito. But you can also check out some of the people in IRC. The channel is #ubuntuph. Pero yun nga lang si ubunTULOG lang ang laging gising sa channel.

We suggest you create also a [Launchpad]("https://launchpad.net") account then magjoin ka na rin sa [Ubuntu Team Philippines]("https://launchpad.net/%7Eloco-philippine-team"). For more information about the team, check out [http://loco.ubuntu.com/teams/loco-philippine-team](http://loco.ubuntu.com/teams/loco-philippine-team).

And oh, this April nga pala (although wala pang definite na date) magkakaroon ng release party ang newest version ng Ubuntu (Natty Narwhal). So stay in touch. Announcements will be made soon.

Welcome sa Forums, sa Ubuntu at sa Linux!


(P.S. I sent this same message to you privately)

Robust and very wide ang acceptance ng Natty, meron mga masaya marami naman ang hindi, pero i'm sure matutuwa ka sa bagong interface.

My name is Rey Tubianosa, from the island province of Siquijor. I started using Linux only last September. When it comes to Linux, all my experience as a Windows network administrator would offer no help. That's why I tried to stay in the forums as much as possible so I can learn the ins and outs of this great operating system. I've been using Ubuntu forums for quite some times but it's only now that I discovered this thread (google-searching solution for my Smart Bro pre-paid kit).

All I can say now is MABUHAY TAYO LAHAT! :lolflag:

### Post by boang311 on 2021-07-27
Mga kababayan.. pwede po patulong? (NOT PRO - just following tutorials in google and youtube)

Meron kasi akong LIVE Server ngayon - mahirap kasi mag explain, hindi ko kabisado ang tagalog :)

example po:


1.  - pinoy.com << (wordpress) main website (naka secured na po lahat https gamit sa libre) letsencrypt 
2. - tracking.pinoy.com << (coded) vhost 
3. - hr.pinoy.com << (coded) another vhost
4. - test.pinoy.com << (coded) for testing purposes

running po ito lahat sa isang [COLOR=#8A6D3B][FONT=&amp]Ubuntu Linux version 18.04.5 
[/FONT][/COLOR][COLOR=#8A6D3B][FONT=&amp]
[/FONT][/COLOR]heto napo yung problema: sakali gumawa po ako ng mirror link sa website ko.. ito na po lalabas

example : somedns.com ---> pinoy.com, ang lalabas po ay si tracking.pinoy.com

--- ano po bah problema dito.. ini-isaisa ko na po tanggal lahat yung vhost dito sa "sites-available"
--- after somedns.com ---> pinoy.com (working)
--- pag ibinabalik ko naman yung mga vhost.. yung babalik narin problema.. 

(non-profit) po pala to :( 


PM PO mga kababayan

---
